{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01EsfLmXc9wDsDRGQzzfKQm6","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"thinking","thinking":"Let me look at the current implementation of `addOrUpdateHost()`. Looking at lines 238-295, I can see:\n\n```cpp\nvoid Cluster::addOrUpdateHost(\n    absl::string_view host,\n    const Extensions::Common::DynamicForwardProxy::DnsHostInfoSharedPtr& host_info,\n    std::unique_ptr<Upstream::HostVector>& hosts_added) {\n  Upstream::LogicalHostSharedPtr emplaced_host;\n  {\n    absl::WriterMutexLock lock{&host_map_lock_};\n\n    const auto host_map_it = host_map_.find(host);\n    if (host_map_it != host_map_.end()) {\n      // If we only have an address change, we can do that swap inline without any other updates.\n      // ...comments...\n      ASSERT(host_info == host_map_it->second.shared_host_info_);\n      ASSERT(host_map_it->second.shared_host_info_->address() !=\n             host_map_it->second.logical_host_->address());\n      ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"updating dfproxy cluster host address '{}'\", host);\n      host_map_it->second.logical_host_->setNewAddresses(\n          host_info->address(), host_info->addressList(), dummy_lb_endpoint_);\n      return;\n    }\n\n    ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"adding new dfproxy cluster host '{}'\", host);\n\n    emplaced_host = host_map_\n                        .try_emplace(host, host_info,\n                                     std::make_shared<Upstream::LogicalHost>(\n                                         info(), std::string{host}, host_info->address(),\n                                         host_info->addressList(), dummy_locality_lb_endpoint_,\n                                         dummy_lb_endpoint_, nullptr, time_source_))\n                        .first->second.logical_host_;\n  }\n\n  ASSERT(emplaced_host);\n  if (hosts_added == nullptr) {\n    hosts_added = std::make_unique<Upstream::HostVector>();\n  }\n  hosts_added->emplace_back(emplaced_host);\n}\n```\n\nThe issue is in the update path (lines 274-276): when an existing host gets a new address, `setNewAddresses()` modifies it in-place. The old address entry stays in the cross-priority host map, creating a dangling reference that causes the memory leak when the host is eventually removed.\n\nThe solution involves removing the stale host from the map first, then creating a fresh LogicalHost with the updated address. Both removal and addition events need to be signaled to the priority set. Additionally, the addOrUpdateHost() method should drop the hosts_added output parameter to streamline the interface. Debug logging should be added to upstream_impl.cc to track cross-priority host map changes, and test expectations need updating to reflect the new per-host notification \"fake_cluster_name\";\n  const std::string host = \"localhost\";\n  const int port = 80;\n  std::pair<bool, absl::optional<envoy::config::cluster::v3::Cluster>> sub_cluster_pair =\n      cluster_->createSubClusterConfig(cluster_name, host, port);\n  EXPECT_EQ(true, sub_cluster_pair.first);\n  EXPECT_EQ(true, sub_cluster_pair.second.has_value());\n\n  // create again, already exists\n of the cluster including adding hosts and removing them.\nTEST_F(ClusterTest, BasicFlow) {\n  initialize(default_yaml_config_, false);\n  makeTestHost(\"host1:0\", \"1.2.3.4\");\n  InSequence s;\n\n  EXPECT_EQ(nullptr, lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"\")));\n\n  // Verify no host LB cases.\n  EXPECT_EQ(nullptr, lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"foo\")));\n  EXPECT_EQ(nullptr, lb_->peekAnotherHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"foo\")));\n\n  // LB will immediately resolve host1.\n  EXPECT_CALL(*this, onMemberUpdateCb(SizeIs(1), SizeIs(0)));\n  update_callbacks_->onDnsHostAddOrUpdate(\"host1:0\", host_map_[\"host1:0\"]);\n  EXPECT_EQ(1UL, cluster_->prioritySet().hostSetsPerPriority()[0]->hosts().size());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"1.2.3.4:0\",\n            cluster_->prioritySet().hostSetsPerPriority()[0]->hosts()[0]->address()->asString());\n  EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[\"host1:0\"], touch());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"1.2.3.4:0\",\n            lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host1:0\"))->address()->asString());\n\n  // After changing the address, LB will immediately resolve the new address with a refresh.\n  updateTestHostAddress(\"host1:0\", \"2.3.4.5\");\n  EXPECT_CALL(*this, onMemberUpdateCb(SizeIs(1), SizeIs(1)));\n  update_callbacks_->onDnsHostAddOrUpdate(\"host1:0\", host_map_[\"host1:0\"]);\n  EXPECT_EQ(1UL, cluster_->prioritySet().hostSetsPerPriority()[0]->hosts().size());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"2.3.4.5:0\",\n            cluster_->prioritySet().hostSetsPerPriority()[0]->hosts()[0]->address()->asString());\n  EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[\"host1:0\"], touch());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"2.3.4.5:0\",\n            lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host1:0\"))->address()->asString());\n\n  // Remove the host, LB will immediately fail to find the host in the map.\n  EXPECT_CALL(*this, onMemberUpdateCb(SizeIs(0), SizeIs(1)));\n  update_callbacks_->onDnsHostRemove(\"host1:0\");\n  EXPECT_EQ(0UL, cluster_->prioritySet().hostSetsPerPriority()[0]->hosts().size());\n  EXPECT_EQ(nullptr, lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host1:0\")));\n}\n\n// Outlier detection\nTEST_F(ClusterTest, OutlierDetection) {\n  initialize(default_yaml_config_, false);\n  makeTestHost(\"host1:0\", \"1.2.3.4\");\n  makeTestHost(\"host2:0\", \"5.6.7.8\");\n  InSequence s;\n\n  EXPECT_CALL(*this, onMemberUpdateCb(SizeIs(1), SizeIs(0)));\n  update_callbacks_->onDnsHostAddOrUpdate(\"host1:0\", host_map_[\"host1:0\"]);\n  EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[\"host1:0\"], touch());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"1.2.3.4:0\",\n            lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host1:0\"))->address()->asString());\n\n  EXPECT_CALL(*this, onMemberUpdateCb(SizeIs(1), SizeIs(0)));\n  update_callbacks_->onDnsHostAddOrUpdate(\"host2:0\", host_map_[\"host2:0\"]);\n  EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[\"host2:0\"], touch());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"5.6.7.8:0\",\n            lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host2:0\"))->address()->asString());\n\n  // Fail outlier check for host1\n  setOutlierFailed(\"host1:0\");\n  EXPECT_EQ(nullptr, lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host1:0\")));\n  // \"host2:0\" should not be affected\n  EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[\"host2:0\"], touch());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"5.6.7.8:0\",\n            lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host2:0\"))->address()->asString());\n\n  // Clear outlier check failure for host1, it should be available again\n  clearOutlierFailed(\"host1:0\");\n  EXPECT_CALL(*host_map_[\"host1:0\"], touch());\n  EXPECT_EQ(\"1.2.3.4:0\",\n            lb_->chooseHost(setHostAndReturnContext(\"host1:0\"))->address()->asString());\n}\n\n// Various invalid LB \n527: void HostImpl::weight(uint32_t new_weight) { weight_ = std::max(1U, new_weight); }\n528: \n529: std::vector<HostsPerLocalityConstSharedPtr> HostsPerLocalityImpl::filter(\n530:     const std::vector<std::function<bool(const Host&)>>& predicates) const {\n531:   // We keep two lists: one for being able to mutate the clone and one for returning to the\n532:   // caller. HostSetImpl::rebuildLocalityScheduler(\n602:     std::unique_ptr<EdfScheduler<LocalityEntry>>& locality_scheduler,\n603:     std::vector<std::shared_ptr<LocalityEntry>>& locality_entries,\n604:     const HostsPerLocality& eligible_hosts_per_locality, const HostVector& eligible_hosts,\n605:     HostsPerLocalityConstSharedPtr all_hosts_per_locality,\n606:     HostsPerLocalityConstSharedPtr excluded_hosts_per_locality,\n607:     LocalityWeightsConstSharedPtr locality_weights, uint32_t overprovisioning_factor) {\n608:   // Rebuild the locality scheduler by computing the effective weight of each\n609:   // locality in this priority. The scheduler is reset by default, and is rebuilt only if we have\n610:   // locality weights (i.e. using EDS) and there is at least one eligible host in this priority.\n611:   //\n612:   // We omit building a scheduler when there are zero eligible hosts in the priority as\n613:   // all the localities will have zero effective weight. At selection time, we'll either select\n614:   // from a different scheduler or there will be no available hosts in the priority. At that point\n615:   // we'll rely on other mechanisms such as panic mode to select a host, none of which rely on the\n616:   // scheduler.\n617:   //\n618:   // TODO(htuch): if the underlying locality index ->\n619:   // envoy::config::core::v3::Locality hasn't changed in hosts_/healthy_hosts_/degraded_hosts_, we\n620:   // could just update locality_weight_ without rebuilding. Similar to how host\n621:   // level WRR works, we would age out the existing entries via picks and lazily\n622:   // apply the new weights.\n623:   locality_scheduler = nullptr;\n624:   if (all_hosts_per_locality != nullptr && locality_weights != nullptr &&\n625:       !locality_weights->empty() && !eligible_hosts.empty()) {\n626:     locality_scheduler = std::make_unique<EdfScheduler<LocalityEntry>>();\n627:     locality_entries.clear();\n628:     for (uint32_t i = 0; i < all_hosts_per_locality->get().size(); ++i) {\n629:       const double effective_weight = effectiveLocalityWeight(\n630:           i, eligible_hosts_per_locality, *excluded_hosts_per_locality, *all_hosts_per_locality,\n631:           *locality_weights, overprovisioning_factor);\n632:       if (effective_weight > 0) {\n633:         locality_entries.emplace_back(std::make_shared<LocalityEntry>(i, effective_weight));\n634:         locality_scheduler->add(effective_weight, locality_entries.back());\n635:       }\n636:     }\n637:     // If all effective weights were zero, reset the scheduler.\n638:     if      const HostsPerLocality& excluded_hosts_per_locality,\n710:                                             const HostsPerLocality& all_hosts_per_locality,\n711:                                             const LocalityWeights& locality_weights,\n712:                                             uint32_t overprovisioning_factor) {\n713:   const auto& locality_eligible_hosts = excluded_hosts_per_locality.get()[index].size()\n716:                                       : 0;\n717:   const auto host_count = all_hosts_per_locality.get()[index].size() - excluded_count;\n718:   if (host_count == 0) {\n719:     return 0.0;\n720:   }\n721:   const double locality_availability_ratio = 1.0 * locality_eligible_hosts.size() / host_count;\n722:   const uint32_t weight =
